Solutions</h2><p>Beyond people counting, gain a visual understanding of the flow of your visitors, while influencing their behavior with improved employee scheduling, location-based campaigns and indoor navigation.</p></div></div><article class="bg-white"><div class="flex flex-wrap md:flex-nowrap items-center justify-start"><div class="w-full md:w-1/2 h-full"><div class="h-full overflow-hidden
